##[$ED11] 1
Statement move_cursor {a$,lst,pos}
				 Select EventCode
						Case	$4c:i=##[$C0A6] (a$):
									 If i Then i=i-1:##[$C08D] a$,pos,lst,i
						Case	$4d:i=##[$C0A6] (a$):
									 If i <##[$C096](lst)-2 Then i=i+1:##[$C08D] a$,pos,lst,i
				 End Select
End Statement
Macro version
	"2.2"
End Macro
#maxhistory=4*8
 Macro check
	CMP.b #"A",D2
	 BCS.w 'JL_0_60E8`@
	CMP.b #"z",D2
	 BHI.w 'JL_0_60E8`@
	CMP.b #"[",D2
	 BCS.w 'JL_0_60E6`@
	CMP.b #"a",D2
	 BCS.w 'JL_0_60E8`@
'JL_0_60E6`@:
	CMP.w D2,D2
'JL_0_60E8`@:
End Macro
Macro newalloc
ADDQ.l #4,d0
MOVE.l execbase,a6
MOVE.l mempool,a0
MOVE.l	d0,-(a7)
JSR -$2c4(a6)
MOVE.l	(a7)+,d1
TST.l d0
BEQ 'lab1`@
MOVE.l	d0,a0
MOVE.l	d1,(a0)+
MOVE.l	a0,d0
'lab1`@
End Macro

				 ##[$C090] lst3,s$,-1,s
				End If
				 ADDQ.w #1,AL_0_8A40
				 !asm
				 MOVEM.l (a7)+,d0/a0
'l15b

tobegin
MOVEQ #0,d0
TST.l 4(a4)
BEQ 'l20
'l10:MOVE.l 4(a4),a4
ADDQ.l #1,d0
TST.l 4(a4)
BNE 'l10
'l20:RTS
addhistory							 ;d0 linenum
.jump_addhistory
 MOVEM.l a0/d1,-(a7)
 LEA history,a0
 MOVEQ #0,d1
 MOVE.w historypointer,d1
 MOVE.l startdisplayline,d0
 ADD.l displayoffset,d0
 MOVE.l d0,0(a0,d1)
 ADDQ.w #4,d1
 CMP.w	#maxhistory,d1
 BLE 'nowrap
 MOVEQ #0,d1
'nowrap:
 MOVE.w d1,historypointer
 MOVEM.l (a7)+,a0/d1
 RTS
historyup
.jump_historyup
 MOVE.l a1,-(a7)
 LEA history,a0
 MOVE.w historypointer,d1
 SUBQ #4,d1
 BPL 'l10
 MOVEQ #maxhistory,d1
'l10
 MOVE.w d1,historypointer
 MOVE.l 0(a0,d1.w),d0
 JSR jumpline
 MOVE.l (a7)+,a1
 RTS
historydown
.jump_historydown
 MOVE.l a1,-(a7)
 LEA history,a0
 MOVE.w historypointer,d1
 ADDQ #4,d1
 CMP.w #maxhistory,d1
 BLE 'l10
 MOVEQ #0,d1
'l10
 MOVE.w d1,historypointer
 MOVE.l 0(a0,d1.w),d0
 JSR jumpline
 MOVE.l (a7)+,a1
 RTS
jump
.jump_jump
 MOVEM.l d2-d7/a1/a5-a6,-(a7)
 MOVE.l a4,olda4
 JSR getword
 JSR tobegin
 JSR addhistory
 MOVEQ #0,d3
'begin: LEA 9(a4),a0
				CMP.l olda4,a4
				BEQ 'nextline
'l5: CMP.b #" ",(a0)
 BNE 'l5b
 ADDQ.l #1,a0
 BRA 'l5
'l5b CMP.w #$8008,(a0)
 BNE 'nostatement
 ADDQ.w #2,a0
 BRA 'l5
'nostatement:
 CMP.w #$8009,(a0)
 BNE 'nofunction
 ADDQ.w #2,a0
 BRA 'l5
'nofunction
 CMP.w #$800d,(a0)
 BNE 'nomacro
 ADDQ.w #2,a0
 BRA 'l5
'nomacro:CMP.b #".",(a0)
 BNE 'l100
 ADDQ #1,a0
'l100: TST.b (a0)
 BEQ 'nextline
 MOVE.l AL_0_E1C8,a1
'l1: CMPM.b (a0)+,(a1)+
 BNE 'nextline
 TST.b (a1)
 BNE 'l1
 CMP.b #" ",(a0)
 BEQ 'do
 CMP.b #";",(a0)
 BEQ 'do
 CMP.b #":",(a0)
 BEQ 'do
 TST.b (a0)
 BNE 'nextline
'do MOVE.l d3,d0
 JSR jumpline
 MOVEM.l (a7)+,d2-d7/a1/a5-a6
'no: RTS
'nextline
	TST.l (a4)
	BEQ 'l20
	ADDQ.l #1,d3
	MOVE.l (a4),a4
	BRA 'begin
'l20
 MOVE.l olda4,a4
 MOVEM.l (a7)+,d2-d7/a1/a5-a6
 RTS
.jumpline
	CMP.l maxlines,d0
	BGE 'ret
	MOVEA.l currsourceline(PC),A4
	JSR cursor_off
	CLR.w column
	CLR AL_0_869C
	JSR gotoline
	JSR cursor_on
	JSR linetext
'ret: RTS
newhelp
.help_win

	FindScreen 0
	##[$C082] 1,?wzdata,30

	##[$C08D] "list",pos,lst.List,pos
	##[$FFC9] ##[$C08A] ("string"),##[$C087],0
	win1=1
 End If
nohlp: !asm
 CLR.b nohelp
 RTS
newhelpmessage
.help_message
	If ev
	Use localstat EventWindow
	Select EventWindow
	Case 1:Select ev
				Case #IDCMP_INTUITICKS
					 str1$=##[$C0A7]("string")
				 If str1$<>str1b$ AND Len(str1$)=>2
							 str1b$=str1$
						##[$C091] lst
						CaseSense Off
						MOVE.l AL_0_8BB4(PC),token(a5)
					While token
						b$=Peek$(token+6)
						If Instr(b$,str1$) ##[$C090] lst,b$+" ;"+Peek$(token+7+Len(b$))
						token=Peek.l(token)
					Wend
						pos=0
						##[$C08D] "list",pos,lst,0
				End If
				Case #IDCMP_CLOSEWINDOW:##[$C083] 1:win1=0
				Case #IDCMP_MENUPICK:
				Case #IDCMP_RAWKEY:
				 move_cursor{"list",lst,pos}
				 Select EventCode
				 Case	$45: ##[$C083] 1:win1=0
				 End Select
				Case #IDCMP_IDCMPUPDATE
					Select ##[$C08E]
					Case "find"
			 Case "list"
						pos=##[$C0A6]("list")
							If ##[$C09B] Gosub startguide
;			 Case "string":a$=i$:i$=Peek$(WZResult)
;					 If i$<>a$
;						WZListRemove lst
;						CaseSense Off
;						MOVE.l AL_0_8BB4(PC),token(a5)
;						While token
;						b$=Peek$(token+6)
;						If Instr(b$,i$) WZListAdd lst,b$+";"+Peek$(token+7+Len(b$))
;						token=Peek.l(token)
;						Wend
;						pos=0
;						WZGadSet "list",pos,lst,0
;					 End If
						End Select
				End Select
 End Select
End If
RTS
startguide:	MOVE.l AL_0_8BB4(PC),token(a5)
.help_startguide

					b$=##[$C092] (lst,##[$C085])
					i=##[$B286](b$,Asc(";"),1)
					b$=Left$(b$,i-2)
						While token
						If b$=Peek$(token+6) Then ##[$80BE] While:Goto found
						token=Peek.l(token)
						Wend

found			 :MOVE.l token(a5),a1
						 LEA searchstring,a0
						 LEA 70(a0),a0
						 MOVE.w 4(a1),9(a0):CLR.b 8(a0):CLR.b 11(a0)
						 OR.b #$80,9(a0)
						 MOVE.l a0,helpsourceline
						 !asm
						 JSR JL_0_FAF0b
						 !basic
Return
newtypenew: !basic
		If win2=0
			win2=1
			FindScreen 0
			##[$C082] 2,?wzdata,20
			##[$C08D] "sort",sort_
			##[$C08D] "const",constant
			If constant=1
				##[$C08D] "string2",cstr$
				Gosub type_listconst
			Else
				##[$C08D] "string2",str2$
				Gosub type_findtype
		a$=""
							 For i=1 To lev:
								 If i>1
										a$=a$+"\"+pos$(i):
								 Else
										a$=a$+"."+pos$(i):
								 End If
							 Next
							 WTitle a$
			End If
		End If
		!asm
		RTS
newtypemessage
.type_message
 If ev

	Use localstat EventWindow
	Select EventWindow
		Case 2:Select ev
			Case #IDCMP_INTUITICKS
				If constant=1
				 cpos=##[$C0A6] ("string2")
				 cstr$=##[$C0A7]("string2")
					 If cstr$<>cstr2$
						cstr2$=cstr$
						cpos=0
						Gosub type_listconst
					 End If
				Else
						str2$=##[$C0A7]("string2")
					 If str2$<>str2b$
							 str2b$=str2$
							 find=0
							 pos2(lev)=0
							 p$=str2$
							Gosub findtype
;						 If find=1
;							 a$=f$
;							 lev=lev+1
;							 MOVE.l newtypebase,d0
;											*nt=PutD0:*nt=Peek.l(*nt):
;											While *nt
;											b$=Peek$(*nt+11)
;												If b$=a$:
;												 *nt2(lev)=Peek.l(*nt+4):
;												 Gosub subtype:find=1:Pop If:Goto f2b
;												End If
;											*nt=Peek.l(*nt)
;f2b:									 Wend
;					 End If
					End If
				 End If
			Case #IDCMP_CLOSEWINDOW:##[$C083] 2:win2=0
			Case #IDCMP_RAWKEY:
			 Select EventCode
				Case	$45: ##[$C083] 2:win2=0
				End Select
				move_cursor{"list2",lst2,-1}
		 Case #IDCMP_IDCMPUPDATE
							Select ##[$C08E]
Case "list2"
			 If constant=0
							CaseSense Off:
							str2$=""
							##[$C08D] "string2",&str2$
							temp$=##[$C092](lst2.List,##[$C085])
							a$=temp$
							lev=lev+1:If lev>13 Then lev=13
							pos2(lev)=0
							find=0
							pos2(lev-1)=##[$C0A6]("list2")
						If lev>1
							i=##[$B285](a$,Asc("."),0)
							i2=##[$B285](a$,Asc("$"),0)
							a$=Mid$(a$,i+1,i2-i-3)
						End If
							MOVE.l newtypebase,d0
							*nt=##[$C0A0]
							 *nt=Peek.l(*nt):
							While *nt
									b$=Peek$(*nt+11)
										If b$=a$:
											 *nt2(lev)=Peek.l(*nt+4):Gosub subtype:find=1:##[$80BE] If:Goto f1a
										End If
							*nt=Peek.l(*nt)
f1a:					 Wend
						If find =0
							lev=lev-1:##[$C08D] "list2",-1:
							a$=""
							 For i=1 To lev:
								 If i>1
										a$=a$+"\"+pos$(i):
								 Else
										a$=a$+"."+pos$(i):
								 End If
							 Next
							 i=Instr(temp$," ")
							 WTitle a$+"\"+Left$(temp$,i)
						End If
				 End If
Case "parent" :
				 If constant=1
					 Else
							 If lev Then lev=lev-1
							 If lev=0
										If str2$<>"" Gosub findtype Else Gosub listtype
							 Else
							 a$=pos$(lev)
							 JSR subtype
							 End If
							 a$="":pos$(lev+1)=""
							 For i=1 To lev:
								 If i>1
										a$=a$+"\"+pos$(i):
								 Else
										a$=a$+"."+pos$(i):
								 End If
							 Next
							 WTitle a$
						End If
Case "sort":
		If constant=1
		Else
			a$=pos$(lev):sort_=##[$C085]:If lev Gosub subtype
		End If
Case "clear":
		 If constant=1
		 cstr$="":
			##[$C08D] "string2",&cstr$
		 Else
			str2$="":
			Gosub type_findtype:##[$C08D] "string2",&str2$
		 End If
Case "const":str2$="":constant=##[$C085]
										If constant=1
											WTitle "Constants"
											##[$C08D] "string2",cstr$
											Gosub type_listconst
										Else
											##[$C08D] "string2",str2$
											Gosub findtype
											a$=""
											For i=1 To lev:
								 If i>1
										a$=a$+"\"+pos$(i):
								 Else
										a$=a$+"."+pos$(i):
								 End If
							 Next
							 WTitle a$
										End If
									End Select
							End Select
			End Select
		 End If
		RTS
.type_listconst
		##[$C091] lst2.List
 If Len(cstr$)=>2
		MOVE.l constantbase,d0
		*nt=##[$C0A0]:*nt=Peek.l(*nt):
		While *nt
		a$=Peek$(*nt+$13)
		If Instr (a$,cstr$)##[$C090] lst2.List,a$+" $"+Hex$(Peek.l(*nt+8))
		*nt=Peek.l(*nt)
		Wend
 End If
		##[$C08D] "list2",-1,lst2.List,cpos
		Return
findtype:
.type_findtype
						##[$C091] lst2.List
						CaseSense Off
						i=0
					 If lev
							*nt=*nt2(lev)
						While *nt
						 b$=Peek$(*nt+15)+" ."+Peek$(Peek.l(*nt+10)+11)
						 If Instr(b$,p$)
							If sort_ Then :i=-1
								##[$C090] lst2.List,b$+"	$"+Right$(Hex$(Peek.w(*nt+4)),4),i:i=i+1
							End If
						 *nt=Peek.l(*nt)
						Wend
					 Else
						MOVE.l newtypebase,d0
						*nt=##[$C0A0]:*nt=Peek.l(*nt):
					 End If
						While *nt
						 b$=Peek$(*nt+11)
						 If Instr(b$,p$) Then ##[$C090] lst2,b$:find=find+1:f$=b$
						 *nt=Peek.l(*nt)
						Wend
						##[$C08D] "list2",-1,lst2,pos2(lev)
						Return
listtype		 ##[$C091] lst2.List:lev=0
		MOVE.l newtypebase,d0
		*nt=##[$C0A0]:*nt=Peek.l(*nt):
		While *nt
		a$=Peek$(*nt+11)
		##[$C090] lst2.List,a$
		*nt=Peek.l(*nt)
		Wend
		##[$C08D] "list2",-1,lst2.List,pos2(lev)
		Return
subtype
		pos$(lev)=a$
		a$=""
							 For i=1 To lev:
								 If i>1
										a$=a$+"\"+pos$(i):
								 Else
										a$=a$+"."+pos$(i):
								 End If
							 Next
							 WTitle a$
		##[$C091] lst2.List
		i=0
		*nt=*nt2(lev)
		While *nt
		a$=Peek$(*nt+15)+" ."+Peek$(Peek.l(*nt+10)+11)
		If sort_ Then i=-1
		##[$C090] lst2.List,a$+"	$"+Right$(Hex$(Peek.w(*nt+4)),4),i
		*nt=Peek.l(*nt)
		i=i+1
		Wend
		##[$C08D] "list2",-1,lst2.List,pos2(lev)
		Return
.click_win
	 !basic
	 TST.w AL_0_8A3E
	 BEQ 'l10
	 FindScreen 0
	 MOVEQ #0,d0
	 MOVE.w AL_0_867C,D0
	 ASL.w #3,D0
	 ADDI.w #$12,D0
	 i=##[$C0A0]
	 MOVE.l AL_0_B776,D0
	 s=##[$C0A0]
	 MOVE.l AL_0_B77A,D0
	 SUB.l #10,d0
	 h=##[$C0A0]
	 ##[$C082] 3,?wzdata,100,i,10,s-i,h,3:MOVE.l remark,d0:remark=##[$C0A0]
	 MOVE.l remark,d0:remark=##[$C0A0]
	 ##[$C08D] "rem",remark
	 ##[$C08D] "string3",str3$
	 ##[$C08D] "all",all
	 clickon=1
	 BRA 'l20
'l10:
	 If clickon=1 ##[$C083] 3:clickon=0
'l20	 !asm
	 RTS
newclickmessage
.click_message:	 Use localstat EventWindow
 If ev
		Select EventWindow
			Case 3:Select ev
						Case #IDCMP_INTUITICKS
								pos3b=##[$C0AC]("list3")
								pos3=##[$C0A6] ("list3")
										 MOVE.l d0,clickpos3
								str3$=##[$C0A7]("string3")
								If pos3b<>pos3c
								 i=##[$C0A5] (lst3,pos3b)
										 !asm
										 MOVEA.l currsourceline,A4
										 MOVE.l d0,a0:JSR clickpos2
										 !basic
								 pos3c=pos3b
							 End If
							 If str3$<>str3b$
								 CLR.l clickpos3
								 pos3=0:pos3b=0
								 str3b$=str3$
								 !asm
								 JSR JL_0_46A0
								 JSR JL_0_466C
								 JSR JL_0_47C8
								 !basic
								 Poke$ ?xtrabuf+8,str3$

							 End If
						Case #IDCMP_RAWKEY
								 move_cursor{"list3",lst3,-1}
						Case #IDCMP_IDCMPUPDATE

								 Select ##[$C08E]
							Case "case"
										str3$="case":##[$C08D] "string3",str3$
										remark=1:MOVE.l d0,remark:##[$C08D] "rem",remark
										 pos3=0
										!asm
										JSR JL_0_46A0
										JSR JL_0_466C
										JSR JL_0_47C8
										!basic
									 ##[$FFC9] ##[$C08A] ("string3"),##[$C087],0
							Case "list3"
										 JSR jump_addhistory
										 MOVE.l windowaddr,d0:i=##[$C0A0]
										 ##[$FFC7] i
										 i=##[$C0A5] (lst3,##[$C085])
										 pos3c=i
										 !asm
										 MOVEA.l currsourceline,A4
										 MOVE.l d0,a0:JSR clickpos2
										 !basic
										 pos3=##[$C0A6] ("list3")
										 MOVE.l d0,clickpos3
										 ;WZPrint "list3",-1,lst3,pos3
							Case "rem"
										remark=##[$C085]
										MOVE.l d0,remark
										;str3$="":WZGadSet "string3",str3$
										pos3=0
										!asm
										JSR JL_0_46A0
										JSR JL_0_466C
										JSR JL_0_47C8
										!basic
									 ##[$FFC9] ##[$C08A] ("string3"),##[$C087],0
						 Case "all"
										all=##[$C085]
										MOVE.l d0,all
										;str3$="":WZGadSet "string3",str3$
										pos3=0
										!asm
										JSR JL_0_46A0
										JSR JL_0_466C
										JSR JL_0_47C8
										!basic
									 ##[$FFC9] ##[$C08A] ("string3"),##[$C087],0
							Case "clr"
										str3$="":##[$C08D] "string3",str3$
										 pos3=0
										!asm
										JSR JL_0_46A0
										JSR JL_0_466C
										JSR JL_0_47C8
										!basic
									 ##[$FFC9] ##[$C08A] ("string3"),##[$C087],0
								 End Select
			End Select
		End Select
 End If
 RTS
hook
 MOVE.l d0,0
 MOVEQ #0,d0
 RTS
JL_0_46D6:
	 MOVE.l d0,-(a7)
	 MOVEM.l a0-a1,-(a7)
	 MOVE.l a1,a0
	 CMP.b #".",-1(a0)
	 BEQ 'sk1
	 CMP.b #";",-1(a0)
	 BEQ 'sk1
	 SUBQ.l #1,a0
'sk1	 MOVE.l expandstore,a1
	 JSR expandline
	 MOVEM.l (a7)+,a0-a1
	 MOVE.l a0,d0
	 !basic
			s=##[$C0A0]
			 MOVE.l expandstore,d0
		i=##[$C0A0]
		s$=Peek$(i)
		If Instr(s$,"Stop")
			 ##[$C089] #WENTRYA_TextPen,2
			 ##[$C090] lst3,"---Breakpoint---",0,s
			 ADDQ.w #1,AL_0_8A40
			 Goto nostr
		End If
		;If Len(str3$)>1 OR remark=0
		 If Instr(s$,str3$)
.click_listadd	##[$C090] lst3,s$,-1,s
		 ADDQ.w #1,AL_0_8A40
		;End If
	 End If
nostr
	!asm
	MOVE.l (a7)+,d0
	RTS
